                       <section>
                        <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/art-in-motion-100-masterpieces-with-and-through-media/">
                         <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                          Art in Motion. 100 Masterpieces with and through Media
                         </h4>
                        </a>
                        <ul class="entry-meta">
                         <li class="entry-meta-author">
                          <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->

                         </span>

                           <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                          </div>
                         </span>
                         <time content="2018-07-15T16:16:17+00:00" datetime="2018-07-15T16:16:17+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">

                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Dal Mediterraneo al Pacifico. Dialoghi attraverso i mari / From the Mediterranean to the Pacific. Dialogues across the seas
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/dal-mediterraneo-al-pacifico-dialoghi-attraverso-i-mari-from-the-mediterranean-to-the-pacific-dialogues-across-the-seas/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>

                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>

                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    [ITA] art*science inizia un programma triennale (2018-2020) sul cambiamento climatico e sul ruolo dell’arte nell’interpretare e rendere consapevoli delle grandi trasformazioni del Pianeta. E per riflettere su argomenti come il “verde”, la “sostenibilità”, il riutilizzo, le energie alternative, l’ambiente, la “Natura”.
 [ENG] art*science starts a three-years project (2018-2020) on climate change and the role of art in interpreting and making aware of the great transformations that our Planet is u...

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/noema-eu-joint-research-center-jrc-ispra/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Noema @ Joint Research Center of the European Commission
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/noema-eu-joint-research-center-jrc-ispra/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-07-08T12:39:52+00:00" datetime="2018-07-08T12:39:52+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     8 July 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-07-24T13:50:46+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/SciArt-at-Noema.jpeg?fit=690%2C518&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="518" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    [ITA] Noema e i progetti a cui ha dato origine sono stati presentati alla Summer School “Resonances” a Ispra, presso il Joint Research Center (JRC) della Commissione Europea.
 [ENG] Noema and the projects originated from it have been presented at the Summer School “Resonances” in Ispra, at the Joint Research Center (JRC) of the European Commission.
                   </div>

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/art-in-motion-100-masterpieces-with-and-through-media/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Art in Motion. 100 Masterpieces with and through Media
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Pier Luigi Capucci
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Pier Luigi Capucci
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/art-in-motion-100-masterpieces-with-and-through-media/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>

                    <time content="2018-07-15T16:16:17+00:00" datetime="2018-07-15T16:16:17+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     15 July 2018

                    <meta content="2018-07-15T16:20:39+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i1.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/cr_reach2_30x40cln_klein.jpg?fit=690%2C431&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>

                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Sat, 14.07.2018 – Sun, 10.02.2019
 Atrium 1+2
 Cost: Museum admission
 
 "Art in Motion. 100 Masterpieces with and through Media. An Operative Canon" will portray the development of media arts by showcasing pivotal pioneering works that utilize technical devices: from photography to cinematography and sound art, the theater of machines and projections, radiophonic and televisual art, the art video, media-based action and Fluxus arts, and the networked and collaborative artistic practices of the ...

                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Towards a Semi-Living Avatar. Investigating the Interface Body-Smart Machines in Stelarc’s Work
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Anna Hatziyiannaki
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Anna Hatziyiannaki
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/towards-a-semi-living-avatar-investigating-the-interface-body-smart-machines-in-stelarcs-work/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-07-01T21:16:23+00:00" datetime="2018-07-01T21:16:23+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     1 July 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-07-08T12:46:06+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/07/06-Amplified-Body-Laser-Eyes-Third-hand.jpg?fit=690%2C457&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="457" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Crossing the boundaries from Cyberpunk Fiction to Reality, Stelarc’s work moves gradually towards the realization of a vision: To investigate the interface between the actual and the virtual world, with the body acting seamlessly in mixed realities, and with an intelligent avatar that performs in the real world, with optical density and tactile experience. This idea, seems to permeate his experimentations with engineering, robotic and digital technology, and with artificial intelligence and biot...
                   </div>

                  <header class="col-lg-4 col-md-4 col-sm-12">
                   <div class="image-holder">
                    <img alt="Text is not Static" class="lazy" data-original="https://noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/zeitraum-640x480.jpg" height="480" width="640"/>
                    <div class="overlay-effect style-1">

                  </header>
                  <section class="col-lg-8 col-md-8 col-sm-12">
                   <ul class="entry-categories">
                    <li class="term-17">
                     <a href="https://noemalab.eu/category/ideas/article/">
                      Article
                     </a>
                    </li>
                    <li class="term-8">
                     <a href="https://noemalab.eu/category/ideas/">
                      Ideas
                     </a>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/text-is-not-static/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Text is not Static
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Jeremy Hight
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Jeremy Hight
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/text-is-not-static/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-06-07T13:33:45+00:00" datetime="2018-06-07T13:33:45+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     7 June 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-07-01T21:15:18+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/zeitraum.jpg?fit=690%2C495&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="495" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Text in its nature and very architecture is anxious, it is neurotic. It is only held in a seemingly apparent stasis. A work with text is never truly finished but ceased. The paragraph is a shivering mass of bent lines as is a single sentence. The systematic function of text is to infer a voice in a code of bent lines and spaces between. The sculptural nature of the lines of letters is akin to an exhibition of forms encoded with implied speech and thought. It also is like the ground awaiting crac...
                   </div>

                     Vital Transformations Mauri Ora
                    </h4>
                   </a>

                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Vital Transformations Mauri Ora consists of three exhibitions, a series of music performances and a hui-symposium. Part of the project involves visually changing the inner city landscape of Nga Motu New Plymouth, which features artist designed vinyl graphics in shop windows and colourful banners hanging from lamposts.
 
 The exhibition Unrealism will take place in a currently unused shop on the corner of Devon and Liardet streets, downtown Nga Motu New Plymouth. It features work by seven Taranak...

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/my-monster-the-human-animal-hybrid/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     My Monster: The Human Animal Hybrid
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/noema/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>

                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/my-monster-the-human-animal-hybrid/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-06-07T12:17:09+00:00" datetime="2018-06-07T12:17:09+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     7 June 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-06-10T12:20:28+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i1.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/MyMonster.jpg?fit=690%2C386&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="386" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    RMIT Gallery
 Melbourne VIC, Australia
 
 29 Jun 11:00am - 18 Aug 5:00pm
 
 Free
 
 Curator: Evelyn Tsitas
 
 "My Monster: The Human Animal Hybrid" explores our enduring fascination and revulsion with the merging of the human and animal, and coincides with the 200th anniversary year of the publication of Mary Shelley’s Frankenstein.
 
 Shelley’s seminal monster novel explores life and death and reanimating flesh. It is also the story of a hybrid outcast, for Frankenstein’s creature was made as a...

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/comunicare-la-scienza-tra-arte-scienza-e-tecnologia/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Comunicare la scienza tra arte, scienza e tecnologia
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->

                   <span class="hidden">

                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/comunicare-la-scienza-tra-arte-scienza-e-tecnologia/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-04-02T11:36:06+00:00" datetime="2018-04-02T11:36:06+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     2 April 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-06-07T13:35:41+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/star_formation.jpg?fit=690%2C507&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="507" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Riflessioni in forma di dialogo sulla comunicazione della scienza, di come "raccontarla” efficacemente e sul possibile ruolo dell'arte, sulle relazioni tra arte e scienza, sui pubblici e sulla necessità di un discorso interdisciplinare.
 Il mondo della ricerca artistica può fornire ulteriori stimoli per alimentare tale discussione? In che modo l'arte può interagire con la comunicazione della scienza?
                   </div>
                   <div class="footer">
                    <a class="read-more style-text" href="https://noemalab.eu/ideas/comunicare-la-scienza-tra-arte-scienza-e-tecnologia/">

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/starts-prize-for-mx3d-joris-laarman-lab-nl-and-giulia-tomasello-it/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     STARTS Prize for MX3D &amp; Joris Laarman Lab (NL) and Giulia Tomasello (IT)
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/noema/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/starts-prize-for-mx3d-joris-laarman-lab-nl-and-giulia-tomasello-it/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-06-06T13:55:36+00:00" datetime="2018-06-06T13:55:36+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     6 June 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-06-06T13:56:01+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/startsprize2018.jpg?fit=690%2C394&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="394" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    The STARTS Prize is being awarded by the European Commission for the third consecutive year. It awards successful collaboration of science and technology with the arts.
 The grand prize in the Innovative Collaboration category goes to a Dutch joint venture, MX3D and Joris Laarman Lab (NL), who have succeeded for the first time in using a 3-D printer to produce a fully functional steel bridge. The recipient of the grand prize in the Artistic Exploration category is Italian interaction designer Gi...

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/calls/spectra-2018-2/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Spectra 2018
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/noema/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/calls/spectra-2018-2/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-06-06T13:44:23+00:00" datetime="2018-06-06T13:44:23+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     6 June 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-06-06T13:44:49+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/spectra_2018.jpg?fit=690%2C395&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="395" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Spectra was originally instigated by artist, Mary Rosengren and CSIRO host partner, Cris Kennedy, following their 2011 Synapse art/ science residency.
 Supported by the Australian Network for Art &amp; Technology (ANAT), Spectra 2012 was held at the CSIRO Discovery Centre in Canberra, and brought together some of Australia’s leading artists and scientists.
 Spectra is now re-visioned as Australia’s pre-eminent art/science gathering showcasing the best research and creative work being produced th...
                   </div>

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/la-complessita-come-problema-sistema-e-risorsa/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     La Complessità come problema, sistema e risorsa
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/la-complessita-come-problema-sistema-e-risorsa/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-05-23T00:11:05+00:00" datetime="2018-05-23T00:11:05+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     23 May 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-05-23T00:17:51+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i1.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/05/attractor.jpg?fit=640%2C559&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="640" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="559" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Pordenone, 23 Maggio 2018
 
 Ore 09:30 - 17:30 presso Consorzio Universitario - Pordenone FVG
 
 Se i problemi che ci assillano: ambiente, alimentazione, lavoro, povertà, salute, sono generati da una rete di fattori che si configurano in modo ricorsivo e sistemico, il pensiero abilitato alla loro soluzione sarà plausibilmente un pensiero anch’esso “a rete”. Il problema è che questo nuovo paradigma cognitivo che, in definitiva, è lo stesso che regola i processi in natura, non ci viene spontaneo m...
                   </div>
                   <div class="footer">
                    <a class="read-more style-text" href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/la-complessita-come-problema-sistema-e-risorsa/">

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/complessita-tra-teoria-ed-esperienza/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Complessità tra teoria ed esperienza
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/complessita-tra-teoria-ed-esperienza/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-04-28T18:39:01+00:00" datetime="2018-04-28T18:39:01+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     28 April 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-04-28T18:39:01+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/04/fesival_complessita.jpg?fit=690%2C330&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="330" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Giunto alla sua IX edizione, il Festival della Complessità è la prima e unica manifestazione nazionale dedicata a far uscire dalla cerchia degli addetti ai lavori il paradigma della complessità e il pensiero sistemico, con l’idea di diffondere idee, libri ed esperienze riconducibili a questo tema in una pluralità di contesti e luoghi.
 
 É un festival libero, autofinanziato e senza scopo di lucro che si svolge ogni anno tra maggio e luglio in decine di città con eventi di vario tipo (presentazio...
                   </div>
                   <div class="footer">

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/perceiving-feeling-interpreting-storytelling-the-art-of-art-science/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Perceiving, Feeling, Interpreting, Storytelling: The Art of Art-Science
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Annick Bureaud
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Annick Bureaud
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/perceiving-feeling-interpreting-storytelling-the-art-of-art-science/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-03-24T15:58:38+00:00" datetime="2018-03-24T15:58:38+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     24 March 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-04-02T11:35:07+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/csm_5_parting_the_waves_5961_B1_54514f69f6.jpg?fit=690%2C345&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="345" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    With Leonardo/Olats, I had the great opportunity to follow the FEAT project. FEAT stands for ‘Future Emerging Art and Technology’. It was an EU funded project during which artists were in residence over 9 months in FET/Future Emerging Technology consortia, FET being one of the cutting-edge scientific research programmes of the European Union.
                   </div>
                   <div class="footer">

 Toronto April 10-12 and Ottawa April 14 2018
 A project by ArtSci Salon

 Community Partners: BYOR Toronto
 
 What is Emergent Form?
 
 Emergent Form is an interdisciplinary multi-part event featuring discussions, performative lectures, performances and guerrilla exhibitions in Toronto (Apr. 10-11-12) ...

                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Spectra 2018
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->

                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="434" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    October 2018 Adelaide, Australia
 
 Spectra 2018 is Australia’s pre-eminent art/science gathering showcasing the best research and creative work being produced through interdisciplinary collaborations between Australian artists and scientists.
 
 Spectra 2018 explores the increasing convergence of art and science and considers how each area impacts the other and how, together, they shed light on who we are and where we’re heading. Taking place in Adelaide, South Australia, the inaugural Spectra ...

                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">

 DIRECTORATE-GENERAL JOINT RESEARCH CENTRE

 Commission européenne, B-1049 Bruxelles / Europese Commissie, B-1049 Brussel - Belgium. Telephone: (32-2) 299 11 11.

                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     SLSAeu Green conference
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>

                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>

                     <meta content="263" itemprop="height"/>

                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    The 12th European Society for Literature, Science and the Arts Conference will be held in Copenhagen from June 13 to 16 2018 with the topic of GREEN. It will be organized conjunctly by the Department of Arts and Cultural Studies, (OU)VERT, and the Faculty of Health and Medical Sciences/Medical Museion at the University of Copenhagen.
 
 The deadline for submissions has been 18 January 2018 - beyond this date, please contact the organizers to check whether your submission can still be accepted.

                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     The New and History – art*science 2017/Leonardo 50 Conference Proceedings
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/pordenone-design-week-2018/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Pordenone Design Week 2018
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/pordenone-design-week-2018/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-03-14T20:41:11+00:00" datetime="2018-03-14T20:41:11+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     14 March 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-03-14T20:46:58+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i2.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/programma2-2.jpg?fit=690%2C535&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="535" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    La VII edizione della Pordenone Design Week consolida il rapporto tra le eccellenze internazionali del design, il campus universitario di Pordenone e il territorio. Un percorso che si snoda in diversi modi: dai workshop dove gli studenti di disegno industriale lavorano per fornire nuovi concept alle aziende locali; passando per i convegni tematici con i massimi esponenti del settore e le innovative lezioni in vetrina: una ricetta che attraverso i negozi del centro storico porta il design ai citt...

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/evolutionary-creativity-the-inner-life-and-meaning-of-art/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Evolutionary creativity. The inner life and meaning of art
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Pier Luigi Capucci
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Pier Luigi Capucci
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/events/evolutionary-creativity-the-inner-life-and-meaning-of-art/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-01-14T02:15:57+00:00" datetime="2018-01-14T02:15:57+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     14 January 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-03-24T16:06:10+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i2.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/01/Evolutionary_creativity_08.jpg?fit=690%2C494&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="494" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Generative art is a key example of a general transformation carried on by many disciplines, which are going to populate our world with increasingly different subjects. [...] In mirroring nature and life, also the generative art forms and processes are leading to the advent of a “Third Life”, the life that little by little humanity is giving to its artefacts.
                   </div>
                   <div class="footer">

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/calls/balance-unbalance-2018/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Balance Unbalance 2018
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->
                     <span class="author-name" itemprop="name">
                      Noema Staff
                     </span>
                    </li>
                   </ul>
                   <span class="hidden">
                    <span class="author-name" itemprop="author" rel="author">
                     Noema Staff
                    </span>
                    <meta itemid="https://noemalab.eu/memo/calls/balance-unbalance-2018/" itemprop="mainEntityOfPage" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/WebPage"/>
                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>
                      <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                      <meta content="599" itemprop="width"/>
                      <meta content="67" itemprop="height"/>
                     </div>
                    </span>
                    <time content="2018-03-06T19:49:49+00:00" datetime="2018-03-06T19:49:49+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     6 March 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-03-06T19:51:59+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i2.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/BUB_logo.png?fit=662%2C789&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="662" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="789" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    Balance-Unbalance (BunB) is an annual International Conference designed around art and design as catalysts to explore intersections between nature, science, technology and society. Every year, the focus is on one or more major current challenges surrounding the ecological crisis and discipline-transcending cooperation.
 BunB 2018 New Value Systems will be hosted September 20th and 21st 2018 by The Patching Zone, the City of Schiedam and partners in Schiedam, The Netherlands. 
 The Balance-Unbala...

                   <a href="https://noemalab.eu/memo/calls/digital-culture-audiovisual-challenges/">
                    <h4 class="entry-title" itemprop="name headline">
                     Digital Culture &amp; AudioVisual Challenges
                    </h4>
                   </a>
                   <ul class="entry-meta">
                    <li class="entry-meta-author">
                     <!-- <a href="https://noemalab.eu/author/plc/" itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person"> -->

                    <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Organization">
                     <meta content="Diginex" itemprop="name"/>
                     <div itemprop="logo" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/ImageObject">
                      <img src="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2017/05/Noema-logo-orizzontale-v5-599x67.png?fit=599%2C67&amp;ssl=1"/>

                    <time content="2018-03-06T19:42:14+00:00" datetime="2018-03-06T19:42:14+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
                     6 March 2018
                    </time>
                    <meta content="2018-03-06T19:51:50+00:00" itemprop="dateModified"/>
                    <span itemprop="image" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/ImageObject">
                     <meta content="https://i0.wp.com/noemalab.eu/wp-content/uploads/2018/03/Conference-on-Digital_Culture_AudioVisual_Challenges.jpg?fit=690%2C306&amp;ssl=1" itemprop="url"/>
                     <meta content="690" itemprop="width"/>
                     <meta content="306" itemprop="height"/>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                   <div class="entry-excerpt">
                    The International Conference on Digital Culture &amp; AudioVisual Challenges will be held in Corfu (Greece) June 1st-2nd 2018, and is hosted by the Department of Audio &amp; Visual Arts (Ionian University).
 
 The call for papers for posters or oral presentation for the International Conference is contained in the attached file.
 
 Deadline for submitting extended abstracts: until April 8th, 2018.
 
 Topics of the Conference include (but not limited to):
 
  	Algorithmic Art
  	Algorithmic music...
                   </div>
